The breakfast had a good variety of Chinese (especially Shanghainese) and western options, mostly on-par with other 5-star hotels in China. Not bad but nothing to make it stand out. 

My complaints are few, but worth mentioning: 1.) the AC in the room just wasn‚Äôt that effective. Even though the weather is cooling down in Shanghai, the room seemed stuffy. posted:Posted May 21, 2024
msg:There are not many choices in South Bund, only Bund Indigo and Wanda Reign. Indigo only has C4, let's talk about Wanda Reign C5. First of all, the basic room is really ordinary, and the view is generally blocked. You can upgrade to the third-level Bund Deluxe Room (the one with a price of 3,000 on Ctrip). There is only one room on each floor, with a wide view. You can see the Bund river view and the city view at the same time, and feel the uneven feeling of the alternation of old and new Shanghai. There is also a massage chair in the room. It is also very pleasant to have a deep massage while looking at the river view.
Let's talk about the design of the hotel. The materials used in the public areas and rooms of the hotel can be seen to have spent a lot of money. It is not ugly. There is a mature and stable feeling. If you think about it, it is a bit similar to the European style under the Chinese aesthetics of the previous generation. A large number of gold-plated faucets and crystal lamps are also very exquisite. It is more suitable for a business style for talking business. The service is pretty good in hotels of this level, and the service of Manager Daisy is particularly good.
The breakfast is not very delicious. The noodles in Songhelou should not taste like this. The quality of bread, vegetables and fruits is average. The swimming pool is a bit small.
The Cool Bar on the 21st floor has a terrace where you can enjoy the best night view of South Bund.
